Data-Coding 7678
Name: EMIS local script codes
Description: Local codes created by EMIS for use in GP prescription data. Codes that have been redacted are represented by negative values.
This is a flat (unstructured) list which uses strings (character sequences) to represent categories or special values.
Coding can be downloaded here as a tab-separated file.
